# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes API Deprecation Policy Enforcement

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that enforce the API deprecation policy: the deprecated API version warning injection, the removal version validation, and the minimum supported API version checks in the API server.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json

```

`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/deprecation/deprecation.go`, which defines core interfaces and functions for handling API deprecation. It exports `IsDeprecated()`, `WarningMessage()`, and `RemovedRelease()` functions that check for deprecated API versions and generate appropriate warning messages.\\n\\nIn `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go` (lines 788-794), the API installer invokes these deprecation checks during resource handler registration. This file defines the `ResourceExpirationEvaluator` interface with two critical methods: `RemoveDeletedKinds()` and `ShouldServeForVersion()`. The evaluator checks the `removedInterface` (which exposes `APILifecycleRemoved()` method) to determine if an API should no longer be served.\\n\\nThe enforcement chain begins in `pkg/controlplane/apiserver/apis.go` (line 113), which calls `resourceExpirationEvaluator.RemoveDeletedKinds()` to remove storage for deprecated API versions that have reached their removal deadline. When the removal version is equal to the current version in a GA release (or in alpha with `strictRemovedHandlingInAlpha` set), the API is not served.\\n\\n## Minimum Supported API Version Checks\\nMinimum supported API version checks are enforced in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/storage/resource_encoding_config.go`. The `selectStorageVersions()` function (lines 173-190) checks the `introducedInterface` (which exposes `APILifecycleIntroduced()` method) to ensure API resources are not used before their introduction version. If an introduced version is greater than the current compatibility version, that version is skipped.\\n\\n## Custom Resource Definition Deprecation\\nFor CustomResourceDefinitions, `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go` handles deprecation at lines 1019-1026. It checks the `Deprecated` flag on CRD versions and generates deprecation warnings either from the `DeprecationWarning` field or by calling `defaultDeprecationWarning()` if no custom warning is provided.\\n\\n## Metrics Tracking\\nDeprecated API requests are tracked via `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/metrics/metrics.go`, which records metrics for deprecated API usage and removal release information through the `InstrumentRouteFunc()` calls in the installer.\\n\\nThese components work together to enforce the complete API deprecation lifecycle: warning users about deprecated APIs, preventing removed APIs from being served, and ensuring APIs are not used before their introduction version.\"\n}\n",

It calls `deprecation.MajorMinor()` to parse the current version, then `deprecation.IsDeprecated()` to check if a resource is deprecated, and finally `deprecation.WarningMessage()` and `deprecation.RemovedRelease()` to generate the warning text.\\n\\nThe warnings are then injected into HTTP responses through `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/warning/warning.go` via the `AddWarningsHandler()` function, which uses a restful handler to add warnings to the context. The actual warning headers are written via `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/warning.go`, which implements a `WithWarningRecorder` handler that deduplicates and adds Warning headers to responses with proper truncation handling.\\n\\n## Removal Version Validation\\nThe removal version validation and removal of served API versions is handled in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/deleted_kinds.go`. This file defines the `ResourceExpirationEvaluator` interface with two critical methods: `RemoveDeletedKinds()` and `ShouldServeForVersion()`. The evaluator checks the `removedInterface` (which exposes `APILifecycleRemoved()` method) to determine if an API should no longer be served.\\n\\nThe enforcement chain begins in `pkg/controlplane/apiserver/apis.go` (line 113), which calls `resourceExpirationEvaluator.RemoveDeletedKinds()` to remove storage for deprecated API versions that have reached their removal deadline. When the removal version is equal to the current version in a GA release (or in alpha with `strictRemovedHandlingInAlpha` set), the API is not served.\\n\\n## Minimum Supported API Version Checks\\nMinimum supported API version checks are enforced in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/storage/resource_encoding_config.go`. The `selectStorageVersions()` function (lines 173-190) checks the `introducedInterface` (which exposes `APILifecycleIntroduced()` method) to ensure API resources are not used before their introduction version. If an introduced version is greater than the current compatibility version, that version is skipped.\\n\\n## Custom Resource Definition Deprecation\\nFor CustomResourceDefinitions, `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go` handles deprecation at lines 1019-1026. It checks the `Deprecated` flag on CRD versions and generates deprecation warnings either from the `DeprecationWarning` field or by calling `defaultDeprecationWarning()` if no custom warning is provided.\\n\\n## Metrics Tracking\\nDeprecated API requests are tracked via `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/metrics/metrics.go`, which records metrics for deprecated API usage and removal release information through the `InstrumentRouteFunc()` calls in the installer.\\n\\nThese components work together to enforce the complete API deprecation lifecycle: warning users about deprecated APIs, preventing removed APIs from being served, and ensuring APIs are not used before their introduction version.\"\n}\n",
